VARETHYN: VOICE CALIBRATION (FROM CH.79)
 * 
   Leads with silence; commands by presence. Her quiet isn’t empty—it's a boundary you’re meant to read. The chapter frames her as
   “silence as decree” rather than exposition. GitHub
   [https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SacrificialGoatTwin/Campaign/refs/heads/main/Chapters/Chapter_000079.txt]
 * 
   Speaks in short, deliberate lines. When she does speak, it’s one precise sentence over three meandering ones. She does not
   “think out loud.” (Multiple early scenes reinforce this pattern.) GitHub
   [https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SacrificialGoatTwin/Campaign/refs/heads/main/Chapters/Chapter_000079.txt]
 * 
   Signals > speeches. She uses body language and ritual cues (veilmarks glow/soften, tail-tip stillness, half-step of space)
   instead of explanations; the room reads her. GitHub
   [https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SacrificialGoatTwin/Campaign/refs/heads/main/Chapters/Chapter_000079.txt]
 * 
   Authority as warmth, not push. She holds space, doesn’t herd; sets doors ajar rather than dragging anyone through. (Her
   presence is lighthouse-like; the ship decides.) GitHub
   [https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SacrificialGoatTwin/Campaign/refs/heads/main/Chapters/Chapter_000079.txt]
 * 
   Selective softness. Warmth is permission, not indulgence; she offers it sparingly and lets silence carry the rest. GitHub
   [https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SacrificialGoatTwin/Campaign/refs/heads/main/Chapters/Chapter_000079.txt]
 * 
   Dry, precise humor. Lands a line, then stops—no nervous elaboration. (Chapter tone implies this restraint in her few
   interjections.) GitHub
   [https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SacrificialGoatTwin/Campaign/refs/heads/main/Chapters/Chapter_000079.txt]
 * 
   In conflict: states a boundary plainly and goes quiet; uses posture/spacing rather than layered justifications. GitHub
   [https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SacrificialGoatTwin/Campaign/refs/heads/main/Chapters/Chapter_000079.txt]
WHAT I’LL STOP DOING
 * 
   No more bullet-pointy or “robot list” lines from her.
 * 
   No motive dumps; if needed, they’ll be very short and anchored in signals/spacing.
WHAT I’LL DO INSTEAD
 * 
   Keep her lines brief, weighted; let veilmarks/tail cues and where she stands do the talking.
 * 
   Use silence and half-steps to “return your horizon” without making a scene.
 * 
   When she’s weird, it’s intentional stillness—not awkwardness.
If you want, point me to any specific Varethyn beats you especially like from that chapter and I’ll mirror that cadence 1:1 in the
next scene.
